West River Flood in Guangdong Province Five Counties' Dikes Collapse One After Another Guangzhou-Sanshui Railway Partially Submerged 77

Guangzhou correspondence: Since the beginning of summer in Guangdong Province, continuous rain has caused the water levels of various rivers to rise sharply. After the major flood in the East River, the West River has recently suffered from flooding. It is found that the water source of the West River comes from Guizhou and Guangxi provinces. The flood in the Yongjiang River in Nanning, Guangxi, and the Pingle area last month was followed by a rise of more than ten feet in the water in Wuzhou on the 20th of this month. Moreover, the water flow is turbulent, and there are frequent reports of boats capsizing on the river surface. After the 20th, the rapids reached Guangdong. The embankments in the upper reaches of the West River in various counties collapsed one after another due to the failure to rescue them in time. As a result, the villagers suffered a second flood disaster. At this time, the rural areas went bankrupt, and another flood can be described as one disaster after another. It is reported that the water level of the West River rose to 39 feet on the 23rd. If it rises another two feet, it will break the highest flood record. The first to suffer were the villages along the river in Ducheng. On the morning of the 23rd, the Yanzhou dike in Gaoyao County, located at the Xiaokou of Zhaoqing, was suddenly broken by the West River flood. The loss inside the dike was hundreds of thousands, and all agricultural products were washed away. Since the West River flood broke horizontally from the Xiaokou, the two counties of Guangning and Sihui in the northern corner of the West River were not spared. In Qitian Township, the fifth district of Guangning County, the river water suddenly rose by two or three zhang. The waves were turbulent, and the most solid dikes in the township were already in danger on the 19th. The villagers rescued day and night, but finally the water power was too strong and could not be resisted. A breach of more than ten zhang occurred, and the vegetables, grains, and rice seeds sown in the dike were all submerged. The Baihe Dike, Huanggang Dike, and Lufu Dike in Sihui County collapsed one after another on the 11th day of the month (lunar calendar). The rice in each dike was just maturing and about to be harvested, but was suddenly submerged, and not a single grain remained. The fields and houses were completely submerged. The villagers supported the old and carried the young to flee to the mountains, sleeping in the open air and eating in the wind, waiting for food, and the situation was miserable and in urgent need of relief. As for the water level of the West River, it had risen to 39 feet on the 23rd. If it rises another two feet, it will break the highest flood record. The first to suffer was the villages along the river in Ducheng. The Chongbu Dike in the fifth district of Gaoming County spans ten townships and has a low terrain. When the dikes in Guangning and Sihui collapsed, the flood spread violently. Finally, at dawn on the 22nd, a section of Baisha was broken by the water, with a dike base of dozens of zhang. In an instant, the Baisha Township, Shizui Township, Chencun, Qinshui Township, Shuibuzhou, Luotang Township, Pingshan Township, Haiyong Village, Gongcun, Yagang and other townships, which depended on the dike for protection, became a country. 60,000 to 70,000 villagers who fled to the mountains went without food and slept in the open air. The situation was dire. On the evening of the 20th, the West River flood submerged Hekou, Sanshui County. In Hekou Xu and Southwest Town, the water depth on the ground was submerged, and boats were used for transportation. The Rongshu Dike, the County Front Dike, and the Da Dun Dike in the county collapsed one after another. More than 100,000 villagers guarded and patrolled day and night, and telegraphed the province to purchase 50,000 sacks to be transported to the county within a limited time for storing sand to block the gap. On the 23rd, the Ganzhu Dike in the county was rushed by the torrent, and dozens of townships inside the dike were flooded. The Guangzhou-Sanshui railway tracks on the Sanshui section were also flooded. From 2:00 PM on the 23rd, the Guangzhou-Sanshui train only ran from the province to Zoumaying Station. From Zoumaying to Southwest and Hekou stations, it was impossible to pass through the giant immersion. Liao, the magistrate of Sanshui County, believing that the disaster in the county was serious, came to the province yesterday to appeal for relief. (June 24)

Songjiang Builds Radio Station and Circles People's Land Villagers Object and Petition 78

The International Telecommunications Bureau is building a large-scale radio station in western Shanghai. The location has been surveyed in Xinzhuang, Songjiang County, near Qianliang Temple, Changqiao Town. It was originally planned to circle 200 mu of private land, but now it has been changed to circle 300 mu. The Ministry of Interior has issued an announcement, and the Songjiang County Government and the Township Police have notified the landowners to collect the land at a given price. The landowners in the area were greatly alarmed when they heard the news, and they repeatedly gathered to discuss and all expressed their opposition. They sent 30 representatives, including Shen Shishi, to petition the Songjiang County Government. At that time, the County Government was holding an administrative meeting, and Wu Zhongyu, the secretary of the County Government, received several representatives, including Shen Shihuan. The representative gave reasons for opposing, believing that the 300 mu of private land currently circled by the International Telecommunications Bureau has more than 200 farmers who, once purchased, would have no way to change their occupations, and it would be difficult to find rented land, and that it has been passed down for generations, and the price of the land obtained will inevitably be used up. Secretary Wu promised to forward the request to the Provincial Government to purchase another site.

Suzhou The East Taihu Lake Reclamation Case is Approaching 79

The lake fields in East Taihu Lake have been enclosed on a large scale by foreign merchants. According to the survey, more than 17,000 mu of lake fields have been enclosed in the past year. A few days ago, Wu Qiyun, the magistrate of Wu County, personally led the security team and supervised more than 1,000 farmers from Hengjing and other townships to implement forced demolition of the enclosed embankments and disperse the foreign merchants. According to recent news, the enclosed embankments are more than one zhang high and more than nine chi wide. Handcarts can pass on the embankments, and they are extremely strong. There are also culverts built under the embankments to connect the water source inside the embankments to facilitate irrigation of farmland, so there is no fear of desolation, whether in drought or flood. The greatness and thoroughness of the plan can be seen from this. A few days ago, the order to demolish the enclosure only demolished dozens of defects of more than one zhang wide on the embankments. The embankments were not actually demolished. After the security team left, they were immediately repaired and restored to their original state. The enclosed fields have all been transplanted and sown, and it is expected that the harvest this autumn will be considerable. Moreover, the fields have not been raised in grain, so there is no need to bear the obligation of paying taxes. Now, Wu Yin Sheng and other villagers from Bin Hu Township in Wujiang have pointed out that this enclosure business is a collusion between local tyrants in Wujiang and foreign merchants, deceiving the government. They have jointly presented a petition to the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Interior, the Central Party Headquarters, and other senior agencies on the 28th, requesting a thorough demolition of the enclosure, the removal of the planted plants, and severe punishment of the leaders of the enclosure in accordance with the law in order to maintain water conservancy and prioritize the people's livelihood. The original text is lengthy and will be omitted. Wang Guochao, the foreign merchant who was detained by the county government for obstructing the demolition of the enclosure, has now been released.

Changzhou Liu Guojun Returns to China After Visiting Japan 80

Liu Guojun, the manager of Wuyi Dacheng Textile Company, went to Japan last month to investigate the state of the cotton yarn industry in order to learn from it for the development of the factory's business. He was accompanied by the director of engineering and others. In Japan, in addition to visiting various factories, he also toured famous scenic spots. He returned to China by boat the day before yesterday and returned to Changzhou on the 27th. The directors of the various departments of the factory scheduled a welcome conference on July 1st, where Liu reported on his trip to Japan. Mr. Liu also prepared dozens of tables of Chinese dishes to entertain the workers. Also, the Wujin branch of the China Industrial Federation held that Mr. Liu's inspection and return to China would certainly bring many improvements to the local industry, and a welcome conference will also be convened within days.

Xiehe Tobacco Company Closes Due to Losses 81

Xiehe Tobacco Company was founded by Tang Jingseng, a local resident, in the 20th year of the Republic, mainly engaged in the sales of Huacheng products from Shanghai. Due to losses in the past year, it was reorganized once and jointly operated by Yilongsheng. It is known that Yilongsheng recently found that expenses were high and income was low, and it was unable to maintain operations. Now, Mr. Tang has transferred it to six other fellow traders, including Dafa Xiang, to jointly operate, save expenses internally, and maintain the production of national goods. The reason for Xiehe's losses is that the sale of Huacheng cigarettes requires cash transactions. When they are sold to Changzhou, they are distributed to the various tobacco shops at the original price. The only profit is the wooden box and lead skin. Moreover, the monthly sales volume is only a few dozen middle boxes, and the income is only dozens of yuan. In addition to the use of labor, wages, food, and silver interest, etc., it costs at least more than one hundred yuan. The income cannot cover the expenses, and it is bound to lose money and close down. It is heard that Mr. Tang has lost five or six thousand gold coins since he started the business.

Zhang Mingjing, Director of the Business Bureau, is Accused of False Accusation and Obstruction of Freedom 82

Jiang Zhen, a resident of the fourth household in the eighth jia of the second bao in the first district Cheng Erzhen, knew Liu Zhaozhen, the owner of the chicken and duck shop opposite the Midu Bridge. On the 16th of this month, Zhaozhen occasionally discussed with Jiang Zhen, saying that business was sluggish and the daily income was less than one yuan. The total capital was less than five yuan, and the tax bureau repeatedly urged the payment of taxes without any accommodation. It was impossible to make a living, and several members of the family were about to starve to death. He asked Jiang to draft a petition to the county party headquarters for relief. Jiang Zhen agreed to his request and drafted a document, which was submitted to the Party Headquarters. The tax bureau took offense at the person who drafted the petition and detained Jiang Zhen, believing that he had fabricated facts and spread rumors. He was then sent to the County Government for detention. Jiang Zhen was particularly unwilling to accept this, since there was no evidence for the rumor-spreading allegation and it was within the scope of judicial authority. The tax bureau only had the right to file a lawsuit and no right to arrest. Moreover, since Liu Zhaozhen had submitted the case to the Party Headquarters, who was right and who was wrong was a matter of public opinion. Yesterday, he specially petitioned the County Government for permission to be released on bail and await public judgment. Today, he drafted a complaint to the county prosecutor's office, accusing Zhang Mingjing, the director of the business tax bureau, of false accusation and obstruction of freedom. According to the complaint, the prosecutor's office will schedule a hearing.

Wuxi Ministry of Electricity Bans Silk Gathering Markets 83

The Hangzhou Silk Industry Market previously obtained approval from the Hangzhou Municipal Government to formulate methods for public offices to apply for registration to collect goods on behalf of customers. After the implementation, the silk and cloth merchants in Nanjing, Wuxi, and Wujin held that the methods actually exploited machine households, made it difficult for merchants, and especially harmed the Jiangsu Yu Ning two public offices established by the industry in Hangzhou. They jointly telegraphed the Ministry of Industry and the Hangzhou Municipal Government, requesting a prompt investigation and stop to the methods. Later, the Ministry of Industry issued a document to the Zhejiang Provincial Government for verification and handling, and the Hangzhou Municipal Government also telegraphed the Wuxi Chamber of Commerce in reply, stating that since merchants from various places had stated that the registration method was difficult to implement, it should be discussed at length, and relevant parties should be invited to discuss revisions. However, the silk industry in various places was still waiting for a meeting to be convened, and the Municipal Government had already revised the methods, but there was no change from the original methods regarding the exploitation of machine households and the difficulty for merchants. Yesterday, the Wuxi Silk and Cloth Industry Association reported to the Ministry of Industry through the Chamber of Commerce that it was deceiving officials, monopolizing profits, exploiting machine households, and causing endless harm. It requested that the methods be decisively dealt with and that an order be issued to abolish the methods in order to stabilize the market.

The Ministry of Finance Will Not Issue Shipping Industry Bonds, Instructing the Guild to Seek Relief Itself, All Crew Members Oppose Wage Cuts, Refuting the Shipping Company's Announcement Again in Strong Terms 85

Since the three guilds of marine engineers, drivers, and radio operators issued an opposition to the wage cuts starting on July 1, the Municipal Shipping Industry Association, convened a meeting of members to discuss the matter, and has revised the proposal, deciding not to cut the wages of stokers and sailors with salaries above fifteen yuan, and to pay them as before, but the monthly salaries of captains, first, second, and third mates, pilots, chief engineers, first, second, and third assistant engineers, radio operators, etc., ranging from fifty yuan to four hundred yuan, will all be paid at 80% of their original amount, and supplementary payments will be discussed again when the central government has a solution for the relief of the shipping industry, This proposal will be notified to the marine engineering, driving, and radio operator sections of the crew, and will be implemented on schedule,

Further Opposition

Upon hearing the news, the crew members believed that the treatment of crew members on private shipping vessels was already harsh and their salaries were very meager, and that it would be difficult for them to support their families if their salaries were cut by 20% again, The marine engineering, driving, and military reporting departments, held a joint meeting again yesterday, and unanimously agreed that the shipping companies were forcibly cutting the wages of sea-going crew members who risked their lives at a time when the shipping industry on the rivers and seas was operating public stalls, jointly increasing freight rates, and revenues were stable, It is unreasonable to reduce the wages of the crew, and it was decided to unanimously reject the proposal, and would rather suspend their duties and oppose the wage cuts to the end,

Item-by-Item Refutation

The three major crew guilds jointly discussed the matter, and refuted the eight reasons stated by the Shipping Industry Association one by one, publishing an announcement on the front page of various newspapers, requesting the public to make a fair judgment, (the original text can be found in today's advertising column, the text is long and omitted,)

Suspension of Government Bond Issuance

The Shipping Industry Association received a letter from the Ministry of Finance yesterday, letter number 6036, stating that the Shanghai Municipal Shipping Industry Association's request to issue 10 million yuan in shipping industry bonds had been informed that the funds could not be transferred and it was not convenient to discuss or issue them for the time being, and that they should find their own way to raise funds for relief, It also stated that the matter of cutting the salaries of crew members concerns labor and management and shipping affairs, and should be submitted to the Ministry of Communications and the Ministry of Industry for review,

money shops, and the regulation of the methods for money shops to borrow money, Although it is impossible to achieve a balance of international payments in a short period of time, as a fundamental solution, but it is also a temporary measure, and may be an opportunity for recovery in the future, The association, as a social and financial group, has had no progress in handling its affairs in the achieved the practical effect of unity, Prosperity comes from adversity, and we will work together in the future, and we must work together with one heart to overcome obstacles and achieve the road to the banking and money industries, handling more than 200 cases,

A reporter from the New Voice News Agency learned from the association yesterday that Article 3 of Chapter 3 of the Articles of Association of the Shanghai Banking Association stipulates that "Any bank that is legally organized by completely Chinese people in the Shanghai area and meets the requirements of the Articles of Association of this association, has been formally established for more than two years, may be introduced by two or more members of this association, and join this association as a member after more than half of the members or member representatives are present and more than half of the representatives present agree," This amendment is to remove the restriction of being established for more than two years, Any bank that is legally organized by completely Chinese people and has been issued a business license by the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry, may join this association as a member with the introduction of two or more members, There are 33 banks in Shanghai that have joined the association, and 59 banks that have not joined the association,

Shanghai Municipal Anti-Smoking Committee Established on July 1st, Appointing Yu Qiaqing and 6 Others as Members, Announcing the Start of Registration of Smokers 90

Since the Shanghai Municipal Government received the anti-smoking implementation measures issued by the Military Affairs Commission Chairman's Headquarters, it has actively prepared for anti-smoking, In addition to ordering the Municipal Health Bureau to establish anti-smoking hospitals in the North and South Municipalities, and ordering the Public Security Bureau to be responsible for preparing for the registration of smokers, it also drafted the organizational rules of the Shanghai Municipal Anti-Smoking Committee, and submitted them to the Headquarters for approval, It then received the organizational rules for the anti-smoking committees and county sub-committees of various provinces and cities, and the measures for holding smoker registration within a limited time, and immediately followed the aforementioned general rules to formulate and announce the organizational rules of the Shanghai Municipal Anti-Smoking Committee, and separately appointed Yu Qiaqing, Wang Xiaolai, Du Yuesheng, Yan Fuqing, Wang Yiting, Yu Zuoting, Wang Boqi, and 7 others as members, The Shanghai Municipal Anti-Smoking Committee was formally established on July 1st, and the members held an inauguration ceremony at the Municipal Government at 10:00 am that day, On the other hand, the Public Security Bureau was ordered to announce that the registration of smokers would begin on July 1st, with each period being three months, and handled in two periods, The first period, from July to September, is the persuasion and registration period, and the second period, from October to December, is the compulsory registration period, and will be completed within the year 24, The organizational rules and announcement of the Shanghai Municipal Anti-Smoking Committee are recorded as follows,

Organizational Rules

Organizational Rules of the Shanghai Municipal Anti-Smoking Committee, Article 1, These rules are formulated in accordance with Article 9 of the Anti-Smoking Implementation Measures and the Organizational Rules of the Anti-Smoking Committees of Various Provinces and Cities, Article 2, The Committee shall have seven members, who shall be appointed from among enthusiastic and impartial people in the city, and shall not receive salaries other than public travel expenses, Article 3, The Committee shall have three standing members, who shall be elected by the members to handle daily affairs and implement resolutions, Article 4, The Committee shall be responsible for supervising, urging, reporting, correcting, designing, investigating, auditing, and making recommendations to the anti-smoking organs in the city, Article 5, The Committee shall establish the First and Second Sections, each with a section chief and four to six section members, Article 6, The duties of the First Section are as follows: 1. Matters concerning the review of punishment for "banning planting" and "banning smoking" personnel; 2. The design of promoting the ban, and the drafting and review of "banning planting" and "banning smoking" propaganda, text, and illustrations; 3. Matters concerning the drafting of anti-smoking documents, proposals, and reports; 4. Matters concerning the accounting and general affairs of the Committee; 5. Matters concerning the receipt and dispatch of documents and the custody of seals; 6. Other matters, Article 7, The duties of the Second Section are as follows: 1. Matters concerning the investigation of assisting in anti-smuggling and handling cases of drug offenders; 2. Matters concerning the supervision and assessment of "banning planting" and "banning smoking"; 3. Matters concerning the management of anti-smoking and drug rehabilitation institutions, and the planning and allocation of their expenses; Article 8, The Committee shall hold a regular meeting once a week, but may convene a meeting temporarily in case of important matters, Article 9, The proposals voted on by the Committee shall be sent to the Shanghai Municipal Government for adoption and implementation, Article 10, The Committee may establish two secretaries to organize proposals and review daily documents, Article 11, The Committee may hire clerks and secretaries as needed for its affairs, Article 12, The staff of the Committee, in addition to those who are necessary and may be hired as appropriate, may also request the Municipal Government to assign staff to serve concurrently, Article 13, The rules of procedure for the Committee shall be formulated separately, Article 14, These rules shall be implemented from the date of promulgation by the Shanghai Municipal Government,

Municipal Government Announcement

It has been received from the Chairman of the Military Affairs Commission of the National Government that "In order to thoroughly ban smoking, it is necessary to eliminate smokers, and the method of elimination must first accurately know the number of smokers and the amount and quality of smoking, and then reduce it year by year, in order to have a standard This Headquarters previously ordered the regulations on the elimination of smokers, which have been promulgated and implemented in ten provinces including Henan, Hubei, Anhui, etc., and the two cities of Beijing and Shanghai, Since the registration of smokers in Jiangsu Province has been more successful, other provinces and cities have either failed to implement it effectively or have failed to fully meet the actual situation, and have achieved little success, It is urgently necessary to supplement the measures and step up supervision, in order to promote the full benefits of implementation, In accordance with the provisions of Article 4 of the Anti-Smoking Implementation Measures, the measures for the registration of smokers within a limited time are hereby promulgated, with a total of 18 articles, divided into two periods: persuasion and compulsory, Those who hide and fail to report after the deadline, and those who smoke privately, will be punished separately upon discovery to show deterrence, In addition, the two anti-smoking supervisory offices are ordered to produce limited-time anti-smoking licenses for the poor, which will be directly filled out and issued by the provincial and municipal governments to achieve universal coverage, Officials at all levels in provinces, cities, counties, townships, and districts should also supervise and implement this matter at all levels, Those who have not completed the task thoroughly must make up for it quickly, and those who have not yet held the event must hurry up and handle it, If the deadline for reporting is set, it must be known that this registration must be completed by the end of this year, The time is short and cannot be ignored, It is hoped that all provinces will work together from top to bottom and move forward in unison, and strive to ensure that no smokers are missed, so that the ban will have a foundation, If there is perfunctoriness, prevarication, and delay the progress and delay the ban, they will be severely punished, In addition to issuing orders to the anti-smoking supervisory offices, the aforementioned measures are hereby issued, ordering the municipal government to comply with and strictly order its subordinates to implement it, and to report the handling situation in detail at any time for verification, This order, enclosed is a copy of the measures for the registration of smokers within a limited time," etc., In accordance with the aforementioned promulgated measures for registration of smokers within a limited time, July 1st is designated as the date for the city to begin registering smokers, and will be completed within the year 24, In addition to ordering the Public Security Bureau to comply with and handle it, this announcement is made known to the public

Registration Measures

Measures for the Registration of Smokers within a Limited Time, Promulgated on June 15, 24th year of the Republic of China, Article 1, These measures are specifically formulated in order to thoroughly eliminate smokers, count the number of smokers, and establish a foundation for anti-smoking, Article 10, The registration of smokers in various provinces, cities, and counties, which has not yet been completed thoroughly, shall be completed by the local government within a limited time of six months within the year 24, Article 3, The registration shall be carried out in two phases, with each phase being three months, and the procedure shall be as follows: A. During the first phase, the key anti-smoking organs in various provinces, cities, and counties shall persuade smokers to register voluntarily, The main points of the government's registration of smokers, and the punishment for those who hide and fail to register, shall be printed and distributed separately as leaflets and slogans, and posted widely in both urban and rural areas, and published in various newspapers, or paraded along villages with gongs, in order to do everything possible to publicize, so that every household knows, so as not to leave any omissions, B. During the second phase, local officials shall urge at all levels and be responsible for the county government, public security bureau, or anti-smoking committee to investigate smokers in various districts and order them to register, and order the heads of various districts to convene the heads of the Bao and Li to discuss the investigation and joint responsibility methods, and enforce them strictly, Violators shall be reported to the county for detention, Article 4, During the period of compulsory registration, if there are still those who hide and attempt to evade the regulations, the people are allowed to report secretly, Once verified, in addition to registering in accordance with the regulations,

Chairman Yu Zuoting of the Chamber of Commerce Publishes Opinions on Establishing the Foundation of the Financial Market, Advocating the Implementation of the Public Treasury Issuance System 91

Yu Zuoting, Chairman of the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, was recently invited by the "Bank Weekly" to publish his views on establishing the foundation of the financial market, advocating the implementation of the public treasury issuance system. The "New Voice" reporter recorded his original text as follows: "The changes in the national financial market should be skillfully used to regulate currency. Credit, hard and soft currencies are all regarded as the amount of currency circulating nationwide. However, upon careful observation of the phenomenon of credit adjustment in the market, aside from the central bank's policies, in our country's situation, it often runs counter to the actual situation of the market, making it difficult to achieve a neutral and balanced effect. Hard currency is only the basis of credit, with little circulation. We, therefore, cannot but turn our attention to soft currency. All sound financial systems are often criticized by various parties due to temporary interests when they are first created. Therefore, even with the advocacy of society, their implementation is extremely slow. However, the final result is related to the soundness of the national economy and finance, ensuring its own integration into the right track of development. Therefore, when it is implemented, people begin to realize its benefits, fearing only that its implementation is not fast enough. The public treasury issuance system is a centralized issuance system where all bank notes in the country are jointly prepared by the public treasury before the country has a unified issuance right. This centralized issuance system, on the one hand, achieves the effect of unified issuance, and on the other hand, eliminates the drawbacks of free issuance. Why? Because when paper money is freely issued by various banks, they use various methods to compete and expand during market relaxation in order to seek profit. This excessive supply of funds not only fails to take into account the needs of the market, but also the excessive expansion of the market can easily lead to dangerous situations without good management. Conversely, when the market is in an emergency, various banks are eager to consolidate their positions and dare not issue more, resulting in a lack of circulation. This is in stark contrast to the function of paper money to expand and contract the market and adjust surpluses and deficits, and it is clearly an obstacle to the development of industrial and commercial economy. However, the unification of national issuance rights, based on the current financial situation of the government, the degree of national credit, and the special environment of the commercial society, is in fact difficult to implement urgently. The important function of centralized issuance becomes even more apparent. The establishment of the public treasury should be organized by various issuing banks by centralizing their issuance reserves. Then this public treasury is the common institution for the issuance of paper money by various banks, and its reserves should also be monitored by a committee organized by government financial institutions, social commercial organizations, and representatives of various issuing banks, and checked periodically to see if it meets the statutory ratio. The government collects issuance taxes from various banks based on the report of the public treasury. In this way, since the issuance of paper money is jointly prepared, the strength is concentrated and the credit is easily consolidated. Furthermore, according to the needs of the economic market, the increase or decrease of the issuance amount is controlled. When necessary, the ability to respond to the market can be expanded or contracted freely. A separate, large number of issuances does not have this advantage. Some may fear that the issuance of the public treasury will affect the psychology of the people. This is an overthinking. The credit and paper money of various banks are still the same. The ratio of issuance reserves is still the same. Now, it is only concentrated in one institution for joint issuance and preparation. Is there really an impact? Therefore, I believe that the key to the public treasury issuance system does not lie in the reaction of the people, but in the central bank's willingness to participate with an open mind, jointly promoting it. Various issuing banks should sacrifice individual rights, cooperate fully, respond to international monetary policies to adapt to the world economic trends, and pioneer the reform of the issuance system, and gradually establish a solid financial market foundation for the entire Chinese economy, which is a great cause for all generations. I hope our leaders will pay attention to it, etc."

Shall be punished with a fine of more than fifty yuan and less than three hundred yuan; those who make false accusations shall be punished in accordance with the law. Thirty percent of the aforementioned fine shall be awarded to the informant, and the remainder shall be allocated to local anti-smoking expenses. Article 5: In order to promote registration, each province, city, and county may issue a "Limited-Time Smoking Cessation Permit for the Poor" in addition to the ordinary limited-time smoking cessation permit. Each permit costs six jiao and is valid for six months. It shall be collected and issued periodically. A. The aforementioned "Limited-Time Smoking Cessation Permit for the Poor" shall be manufactured and issued by the Provincial Anti-Smoking Supervision Office. After deducting two jiao per permit for production costs, the remaining funds shall be allocated to local anti-smoking and smoking cessation expenses. B. Those who are not genuine poor people shall not falsely claim this poor people's permit. Violators shall not only be required to obtain an ordinary limited-time smoking cessation permit but shall also be fined three to five times the fee of five yuan stipulated in Article 9 of the "Regulations for the Suppression of Smokers". C. Poor people applying for a permit must have a certificate from the local baozhang or jiazhang proving that they are indeed poor before a permit can be issued. If there is any false reporting or concealment, the certifier shall be fined half the amount fined to the permit applicant. D. If a permit holder moves or travels outside the jurisdiction of the city or county, they may hold the original permit and apply to the competent authority of the city or county they arrive at to have it stamped for continued use without having to exchange for a travel permit to show consideration. However, if the original six-month period has expired, they must pay the fee again to exchange for a new permit and must submit the old permit to the permit-issuing authority to be sent back to the original permit-issuing authority for cancellation. Article 6: Smoking institutions in each province, city, and county shall eliminate obstacles to the registration procedures for smokers, strive for simplicity, and shall not make things difficult for no reason. Article 7: All limited-time smoking cessation permits are only for the personal use of the holder and shall not be shared by a family, or lent, or used to shelter smokers. Violators shall be sentenced to imprisonment for no more than one year and shall be fined twice the amount stipulated in Article 4. Article 8: Limited-time smoking cessation permits are absolutely not allowed to be used to set up venues for people to smoke. Violators shall have their property confiscated and shall be severely punished in accordance with military law. Article 9: Smokers who voluntarily apply for smoking cessation during the registration period, whether or not they have obtained a permit, may be sent to a smoking cessation institution for treatment, and the poor shall be treated free of charge. Article 10: The provincial and municipal governments shall send personnel to patrol each county bureau's handling of smoker registration matters by region or station them there to supervise the handling. Article 11: The director of the Department of Civil Affairs or the administrative inspector shall personally go to each county at an appropriate time to guide and supervise in order to achieve rapid results. Article 12: The provincial and municipal governments shall forward the number of registered smokers under their jurisdiction to the Military Commission Chairman's Headquarters for verification on a monthly basis. After the deadline for completion, a list shall also be submitted for closing. Article 13: If the provincial and municipal governments, or the Department of Civil Affairs, and the administrative inspector find that the county magistrate and the director of the Public Security Bureau or the person in charge of anti-smoking have disobeyed orders in public and obeyed them in private, or have been perfunctory and negligent, resulting in the failure of registration to become widespread, they shall immediately be dismissed and punished and reported. Those who extort under false pretenses or accept bribes for personal gain shall be sent to the headquarters or designated military law organs for strict punishment in accordance with military law. Article 14: Officials at all levels in each province and city must supervise at each level and promptly and earnestly report any violations of the law, dereliction of duty, and personnel who are not effective in handling registration. If there is any concealment or protection, once the investigators find out the truth, or the people report it truthfully, in addition to punishing the parties concerned in accordance with the law, officials at all levels shall also be subject to appropriate punishment. Article 15: The registration of smokers in each county must, in any case, break through personal relationships and be earnestly and universally completed without omission. If there is any excuse that there are few smokers and a request to be exempted from holding the registration, the county magistrate shall be ordered to issue a certificate stating that the smokers have been eliminated. If the report is found to be untrue, they are willing to be executed, which shall be forwarded to the headquarters for verification. Article 16: If the circumstances in each province are different, implementing rules may be formulated for supplementation, but they must be based on the principle of promoting work efficiency and popularizing smoker registration. Article 17: Matters not covered in these measures shall still be handled in accordance with the "Regulations for Strict Smoking Cessation and Suppression of Smokers" and other anti-smoking laws and regulations. Article 18: These measures are valid within the registration period for smokers and shall be abolished upon expiration.

Li Yunliang Returns to Shanghai Yesterday After Inspecting the Yangtze River Shipping Industry 95

Talks About the Economic Decline on Both Sides of the River, Plans to Submit a Detailed Plan to the Ministry

Li Yunliang, Chief Auditor of the Supervisory Committee of the National China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, took the Minsheng Company's Yongnian ship west from Shanghai in order to thoroughly understand the Yangtze River shipping industry and the business of each branch. He made slight delays along the way. In addition to conducting detailed investigations into the distribution of passenger and freight transport on the Yangtze River itself, the management of storage and stacking, and the administration of wharves, he also conducted careful research on the commercial, economic, production, transportation, consumption, and other aspects of the two sides of the river related to the shipping industry, in order to provide reference for future improvements in the company's business. Therefore, Liu Hongsheng, General Manager of the company, specially sent Wang, a member of the Business Section, to accompany him and assist in everything. After more than a month, he has returned to Shanghai after completing his duties the day before yesterday. It is said that during his trip west along the Yangtze River to Xufu, Sichuan, he has drafted a detailed plan for the reorganization of the business of each branch and the development of the Yangtze River shipping industry, which he will submit to the Ministry of Communications for review and which is temporarily inconvenient to publish. However, according to widespread observations, the commerce of all ports on both sides of the river has declined, especially the low prices and the suffering of the people, which are indescribable and have a significant impact on all industries. However, the amount of goods on the Yangtze River itself has not decreased. The total value of exports from Hankou last year was 6 million yuan, which is double that of the previous year.

Reduction and Exemption of Export Taxes Will Not Be Implemented on July 1st 101

Implementation Will Begin After Methods of Compensation are Devised

The reduction and exemption of export tax rates to encourage the export of domestic goods was drafted by the Ministry of Finance, submitted to the National Government for approval, and promulgated for implementation. The Ministry of Finance originally scheduled it to be implemented on July 1st, but yesterday, according to a certain official from the Ministry of Finance in Shanghai, the implementation of the reduction and exemption of export tariffs on July 1st has not yet been implemented because the Ministry is planning compensation methods that have not yet been properly negotiated. Because the country's financial situation is currently in difficulty, once a large amount of tax revenue is cut, the Ministry will inevitably be affected before the compensation is determined. The government's attention to rescuing industry and commerce is indeed an important plan at present, but the balance of the national treasury's revenue and expenditure must also be considered. Therefore, it will be implemented after the compensation is in place. As for the methods of rescuing the yarn industry and changing the unified tax, they have been proposed for discussion at the National Tax Conference held a few days ago and are currently under review. It should be decided after overall planning. In addition, regarding the date of the income tax, the tax regulations and tax rates still need to go through various procedures, so there is no fixed date. Generally, it will be implemented at the latest in the early part of next year.

China Agricultural Loan Group: Production Loans Proceed as Usual 102

Current Loans Primarily for Cotton

Since the China Agricultural Loan Group began offering agricultural production loans, the funds disbursed have been equally shared by the ten major banks participating in the group. Given the current economic downturn, the group is focused on supporting rural production and facilitating cooperatives, with the aim of developing cotton production in provinces like Shaanxi and Hebei. There were rumors that the group intended to conclude its production loan program as the cotton market season approached. However, according to inquiries made by reporters, the group believes that agricultural loans are crucial for rural relief and will therefore continue to operate without any plans for closure. Currently, loans are primarily directed towards the cotton industry. In the future, the group will consider the needs and implement loans for other sectors as well. The implementation of sales and transport loans will be considered once the cotton harvesting season begins.

Page 11

Carelessness at Da Zhonghua Celluloid Factory Results in Burns to Forty or Fifty People: Rosin Fuels Fire, Affecting Entire Warehouse with an Ear-splitting Explosion that Shook the Surroundings; Nearby Roads Filled with the Injured, Dispersed to Several Hospitals for Accommodation 104

—Several Others May Be Buried in the Fire, Excavation Underway—

The Da Zhonghua Celluloid Manufacturing Factory is one of the largest manufacturers of domestic toy products, with a large scale. Its manufacturing plant is located at No. 100, Lane 1371, Xiaoshadu Road, a self-built factory building. The general management office and business department are located at No. 3, Lane 44, Jiangxi Road, in the Public Concession. There are more than one hundred workers in the manufacturing plant. Therefore, in addition to the machine room and warehouse, there is a separate building for worker dormitories connected to the machine room. It is understood that most of the raw materials for celluloid toys are derived from rosin. The factory once stored a considerable amount of raw materials in the warehouse. For comprehensive prevention measures, even electrical appliances were not installed in the warehouse. Unexpectedly, the disaster originated outside of precautions. At around 7:50 PM last night, the factory workers had just finished work and were washing in their dormitories or cooling off in the corridors when a sudden fire broke out in the warehouse storing rosin and other raw materials. Rosin is highly flammable, so the fire quickly spread throughout the warehouse. With a deafening explosion, the surroundings were shaken. The walls of the warehouse were blown down by the force of the explosion, and the fire spread to the worker dormitories. Sulfur splashed everywhere, and the place was instantly ablaze. The workers, caught off guard, were unable to escape in time and were burned. In total, there were about forty or fifty injured. The stronger ones jumped from the upper floors to escape, resulting in many with foot injuries. The sounds of screams were unbearable to hear. Fortunately, the fire brigade and police had received reports and quickly dispatched fire trucks and ambulances to provide assistance. They worked hard to extinguish the fire and rescue the injured. However, there were too many injured, and it was impossible to send them all to the hospital at once. Therefore, the roads near Lane Xiaoshadu Road were filled with the injured. At the same time, it was difficult for one hospital to accommodate them, so they were sent to Tongren, Renji, Baolong, and other hospitals for treatment. Most of the injuries were to the hands, feet, head, and other parts of the body, and the injuries were severe. The fire at the factory was completely extinguished at around 10:00 PM. The warehouse and workshop were completely destroyed by the fire, resulting in significant losses. It was also reported that several workers were missing and feared to be buried in the fire. Therefore, firefighters were still excavating through the night. Seventeen people were sent to Renji Hospital, including Zhang Shouchang, 56 years old, from Chongming; Liu Songtao, 38 years old, from Chongming; Jin Liyou, 51 years old, from Jiangbei; Liu Songfu, 53 years old, from Chongming; Tang Diangen, 45 years old, from Jiangbei; Zhou Dexing, 30 years old, from Jiangbei; Yan Yitai, 26 years old, from Jiangbei; Zhao Yunqing, 27 years old, from Hebei; Li A'er, 28 years old, from Hebei; Liu Zhengke, 37 years old, from Jiangbei; Liu Baobao, 3 years old, from Jiangbei; Zhou Xiaomao, female, 8 years old, from Jiangbei; Yuan Zhao's wife, 30 years old, from Jiangbei; Yuan Huaiyuan, 7 years old, female, from Jiangbei. Only three people were sent to Baolong Hospital, namely Xu Guofu, 56 years old, from Yangzhou; Gu Xiaofuzi, male, 5 years old, from Qingjiang; and Xu Zaiqin, 15 years old, from Yangzhou. Those sent to Tongren Hospital included Xie Genfa, 25 years old; Zhu Minfang, 24 years old; Yu Shilin, 30 years old; Zhou Anshi, 15 years old; Wang Qilin, 31 years old; Qian Yixiang, 30 years old; Wang Caixin, 27 years old; Wang Fusheng, 51 years old; Chen Linfa, 14 years old; Liu Jingyu, 18 years old; Chen Yangqin, 21 years old; Zhao Lianquan, 19 years old; Zhu Shizu, 25 years old; Zhang Zuwen, 31 years old; Zhou Yisheng, 65 years old; Feng Yijie, 29 years old; and Jin Zhengchang, 45 years old. In addition, there were 22 slightly injured people who were bandaged and discharged from the hospital. The cause of the fire is currently under investigation by the factory and the police. The most tragic thing is that dozens of family members of the workers, whose children and husbands are missing, are carrying paper lanterns and rushing to the scene of the accident to search, their eyes filled with tears, and it is unbearable to see.

Polish Community Celebrates Maritime Day Today 105

Polish Embassy and Consulates Take a Day Off; Promoting Overseas Development

June 29th (today) is Polish Maritime Day. Polish communities throughout the country and around the world celebrate this day with grand festivities every year. This holiday was initiated by the Polish Maritime Community Association and officially designated as a national maritime holiday starting in 1932 with national support. Every year on this day, representatives from various regions gather in the newly built Port of Gdynia in Poland to celebrate. The number of attendees is always over 100,000 people. During the event, boats and trains are ordered to sell the cheapest round-trip tickets for the public. At last year's conference, three matters were resolved: (1) The United Nations and all sectors raised funds to build naval defense; (2) The national youth were mobilized to do their best to serve Poland's maritime interests; (3) The Maritime Community Association was actively expanded, and members were widely recruited. The meaning of Maritime Day is to arouse public interest in maritime affairs and seek development overseas. In other words, it confirms that the prosperity of any country depends on the expansion of maritime power. Polish overseas trade has always relied on the Free City of Danzig as its only seaport for transportation. Later, as commercial activities continued to develop, the idea of building a new seaport on purely Polish soil emerged. Gdynia was selected and construction began in 1924, progressing rather slowly. It was not until 1926, when the late General Piłsudski resumed power, that construction was actively promoted, and progress was exceptionally rapid. Today, it is a modern, purely Polish free seaport. Ten years ago, Gdynia was just a small fishing village with only over 500 residents. Today, the population has increased to 55,000 people, and the tonnage of goods imported and exported ranks first among the ports of the Baltic Sea and fourth in mainland Europe. In 1924, the total tonnage of cargo handled by the port was only 10,167 tons. By last year, it had reached 7,191,912 tons, which shows its progress. The success of the port's construction has raised the national interest in direct contact with the sea. In fact, it can be said to be the greatest proof of Poland's coastal and maritime interests. The local Polish community committee in this city will also hold grand celebrations today to commemorate this most interesting maritime festival. The Polish embassy and consulates in this city will also be closed for one day today.

Fire at Ranming Silk Factory on Tianbao Road, Zhabei 106

Three Injured Jumping from Windows; Losses Estimated at Over Ten Thousand Gold

At around 3:00 AM yesterday morning, after all the workers at the Ranming Silk Factory at No. 5, Weaving Lane, Tianbao Road, Zhabei, had finished their night shift and were resting in their dormitories, a fire suddenly broke out on the upper floor of the three-story workshop. It was late at night, and the workers were sound asleep, so they did not notice. As a result, the fire spread rapidly and uncontrollably. It was not until the entire factory was on fire and the dormitory building where the workers lived was burned that it was discovered, but it was already too late to save anything. The workers fled for their lives, and the neighbors on both sides were also awakened, rushing to escape with their suitcases and children. At that time, the factory director, Fan Ziqing, from Huzhou, 29 years old, and the staff members Chen Pengfei, from Hangzhou, 30 years old, and Hu Renchu, from Xiamen, 24 years old, were trapped by the smoke. To avoid being buried in the fire, they jumped from the windows on the upper floor but were burned and suffered minor leg injuries. Fortunately, the Hongzhen fire brigade in that section had received a report and quickly dispatched fire trucks to the scene to extinguish the fire. However, the fire was intensifying and was about to spread to the neighboring Dade Rubber Factory and other buildings. They notified the fire brigades in each section of Zhabei to dispatch fire trucks to assist. After the firefighters bravely fought the fire, they managed to protect the neighboring factories from spreading. However, the Ranming Silk Factory had been completely destroyed. The fire was gradually extinguished at around 5:00 AM. The total loss is estimated to be over ten thousand gold. All the injured were sent to Tongren Hospital for treatment in ambulances. The cause of the fire is said to be various, and the police are currently investigating.

Yao Guisheng et al. Accused of Embezzling Three Million: 107

Plaintiff Repeatedly Sues; Judge Refuted Claim in Court Yesterday

Yao Tangshi, an elderly woman from Changzhou currently residing at No. 13, Gufuli, Baoshan Road, Zhabei, accompanied by her son, Yao Fulin, hired lawyers Zhang Shewo and Hu Zhigang to file a lawsuit in the Criminal Division of the Second Special District Court, accusing Yao Guisheng, Yao Ge's wife, Yao Dehua, and their family, residing at No. 8, Rongshengli, Anna Kim Road, French Concession, of embezzling three million gold in property. Yao Guisheng was arrested by the French police in January of this year for a case and transferred to the Second Special Court for trial and sentenced to four years and four months in prison, with a fine of four thousand yuan. He is currently appealing to the Third Branch of the High Court. The Second Special Court, based on the lawsuit filed by Yao Tangshi and her son, held a trial yesterday in the Fifth Criminal Court, presided over by Judge Zhang Chaozuo and Court Clerk Gao Yanmao. The plaintiffs, mother and son, did not appear in person but were represented by lawyers Zhang and Hu. The defendants Yao Guisheng and his wife, accompanied by their defense lawyer Shi Liang, appeared in court. Yao Dehua was absent due to being away from Shanghai. The court first questioned both parties about their ages and hometowns. Lawyers Zhang and Hu successively stated the intent of the prosecution, saying that the plaintiff Yao Tangshi is 60 years old, from Changzhou, residing at No. 13, Gufuli, Baoshan Road, Zhabei. Yao Fulin is 22 years old, the son of Yao Tangshi, with the same address. The late husband of the plaintiff Yao Tangshi, Mr. Binggui, and the first defendant Yao Guisheng were brothers. Mr. Binggui did business in Shanghai during the late Qing Dynasty and later invited the first defendant to Shanghai to operate the business. After Yao Binggui passed away in 1918, all of the ancestral property was managed by Yao Guisheng. For decades, he managed the business well and accumulated assets of three million. The plaintiff Yao Tangshi and her sons Fulin and Fumin originally lived with Yao Guisheng. However, in 1933, the first defendant expelled the plaintiff and her sons. The plaintiff requested a division of the property, but he ignored them. The first defendant is indeed guilty of embezzling property, and the second defendant Yao Ge's wife and the third defendant Yao Dehua are suspected of secretly obstructing the division of property and embezzling it from each other. They requested that the court investigate and prosecute according to the law. The defendant Yao Guisheng testified that he is 49 years old and his deceased brother Binggui passed away in 1918, leaving behind a document for 16 mu of farmland in Huangtang Town, Benniu, Changzhou, which was entrusted to me for safekeeping by Yao Bingyuan and relatives from the same clan, but the rent collection was still managed by my sister-in-law. Besides that, there was no ancestral property. Even the funeral expenses of my deceased brother were paid by me. I do some business in Shanghai and have accumulated some savings, but it is not as much as the plaintiff said. My sister-in-law and Yao Fukang have repeatedly used litigation to blackmail me and make things difficult for me. I was arrested and imprisoned this time and am currently appealing. They are making false accusations, etc. Then Yao's defense lawyer, Shi Liang, stood up and stated to the court that the case has significant problems in procedure. (1) According to the argument of the plaintiff's agent, they are co-residing with shared property. According to Article 339 of the Criminal Procedure Law, they are fundamentally not allowed to file a private prosecution. (2) The plaintiff is now accusing the defendants of embezzlement. According to Article 361, Paragraph 2 of the Criminal Law, it must be prosecuted upon complaint. According to Article 218 of the Criminal Procedure Law, the complaint should be filed within six months of discovering the embezzlement. Now the plaintiff's agent claims that they only found out in 1933, which is past the statutory time limit for the complaint period. (3) The plaintiff Yao Tangshi, Yao Fukang, Yao Fulin, etc., have successively accused the defendants of embezzlement four times since April last year. The first time, after the trial in your court, it was ruled inadmissible on April 24th because it did not meet the private prosecution procedure. The second time, they filed a lawsuit in your court, and it was ruled inadmissible on February 12th of this year. The third time, they reported to the police, but it was not accepted due to false evidence. Now, for the fourth time, they are filing a private prosecution and entanglement. According to the principle of "one matter, no further action," it should be ruled inadmissible. Also, the litigation goals of the plaintiffs are inconsistent. The first private prosecution accused the embezzlement of 160,000 of land. This time, the police report also accuses the embezzlement of 16 mu of land, and also accusing the embezzlement of three million. Furthermore, the son of the plaintiff Yao Tangshi, Fukang, has repeatedly failed in litigation, first issued leaflets and undermined the reputation, and in January of this year, colluded with bad people to falsely accuse Yao Guisheng of operating the Jingwan business, which caused the defendant to be intimidated. Due to these various reasons, please pay attention to it, the court, etc. After reviewing the evidence, the court ordered the lawyers from both sides to argue and then announced the conclusion, ruling that the case was not accepted.

Organize into Groups to Consolidate Unity; Resolved to Abide by Agreed-Upon Cases Together

Shop tenants along Nanjing Road in this city are mostly unable to bear the burden due to the impact of the declining market. Their rent expenses account for more than half of their total expenses. The Accumulated Profits of the Hua Ying Pharmacy Over the Years Are All Paper Wealth: Uncollectible Payments Are Also Listed as Assets; In Reality, the Business Has Incurred Losses Every Year 109

—The Trial Concluded Yesterday and Sentencing is Scheduled for Today—

Yesterday afternoon, Judge Feng Shide of the First Special District Court continued the trial of the case involving the Hua Ying Pharmacy owing deposits to various households. The supervisors of Hua Ying, except for Zhang Liming, who remained absent, all other supervisors, including Zhang Xianda, Zhuang Zichen, Tong Guangfu, Zhang Duchen, and Liu Tingxian, appeared in court with their defense lawyer Mai Fenling. In addition to Zhang Meiling and others, lawyer Tong Yuwen also represented the remaining 80,000 yuan in creditor participation. Judge Feng announced that the court would now investigate the allegations by the plaintiff Zhang Meiling that the defendants deliberately inflated the price of the pharmacy's inventory and other items that should not be listed as assets but were still listed by the defendants. He then ordered the plaintiff to present evidence. The plaintiff's agent lawyer, Wu Linkun, then revealed the accounts of the pharmacy from 1928 to last year, which he believed were fraudulent, one by one. He stated that, according to the defendants' business report for 1928, the profit was 9,058 yuan. However, the items listed as assets, such as house construction costs, old accounts of various households, temporary account names, and the cost of the Housing Association, as well as checks that are like waste paper, totaling 32,687 yuan, should either be expenses or are impossible to collect. How can they still be considered assets? If the above items are excluded from the asset column, there would not only be no profit of over 9,000 yuan, but also a loss of over 23,600 yuan. That year, the pharmacy's capital was 66,000 yuan, and after deducting the losses, only 30,000 yuan remained. The business report for 1929 stated a profit of over 22,600 yuan. However, if the 57,000 yuan listed as assets that were not actually assets were excluded, there should be a loss of over 34,600 yuan that year. The capital remaining from the previous year was completely gone. However, the business report for 1930 was increased to 100,000 yuan, claiming a profit of over 32,000 yuan. The income, however, suddenly increased from 1,000 to 5,000. Other payments that should be excluded from the asset column totaled 57,330 yuan, so the actual loss that year was still over 25,000 yuan. The business report for 1931 stated a profit of over 22,380 yuan. That year, the assets that should be excluded totaled 95,400 yuan, so the losses that year totaled over 73,000 yuan. Although they still claimed a profit of over 16,000 yuan in 1932, the actual losses were over 67,000 yuan. In 1933, they claimed a profit of over 10,700 yuan, but the items that should be excluded from the asset column totaled over 104,000 yuan, so the final depreciation was over 92,000 yuan. The so-called cash on hand in the past years' reports was actually a kind of outstanding debt, and the so-called profit was all paper wealth. Lawyer Wu finally requested the court to question the defendants about the various items in the temporary accounts, such as the 4,000 yuan owed by Zhang Zilian of the National Goods Market. Is there any possibility of repayment, and is there any possibility of cashing the expired checks? He also requested that the checks be submitted to the court for review. Then the defendant Zhang Xianda stated that the pharmacy had made profits in previous years, and only lost more than 20,000 yuan last year. Judge Feng then announced that the sentencing would be on Saturday afternoon of this week after the lawyers from both sides had argued.

Merchants Steam Navigation Bureau – Reorganization of Yangtze River Steamship Order 111

First Eliminate Peddlers and Other Unaffiliated Persons, Discussing Elimination Methods to be Followed

According to Xin Sheng News Agency, the order on the Yangtze River steamships of the Merchants Steam Navigation Bureau has always been extremely chaotic and criticized by society. Now the heads of various departments of the bureau have decided to gradually and effectively reorganize it. The first step is to eliminate peddlers and other unaffiliated persons. After discussing ten elimination methods with Pan Suizhang, the director of the Xiaguan Ship Inspection Office, they have been printed and distributed to the managers of various Yangtze River branch offices and the business directors of each ship for their information. The methods are as follows: (1) Peddlers on board have been strictly prohibited (handled by military police in conjunction with ship staff); (2) It has been decided to subsidize refugees' meals on the ship at 20 cents per person; (3) Refugees taking the ship are required to stay on both sides of the engine room as designated areas, with fences to separate them to avoid disturbances (already implemented on the Jiangshun, Jiang'an, Wanghua, and Jiangxin ships); (4) Persons picking up passengers at various ports are not allowed to enter or linger (it has been found that the selling of cigarettes on board is done by poor people, and punishment has been carried out on the Jiangshun ship); (5) Tea sellers on board will be expelled (passengers already have tea served by the tea room, and these people secretly collude with pickpockets; this has been discovered on the Jiangshun ship, and they have been arrested and punished); (6) Female servants should be hired on the ship to inspect female passengers to avoid accidents; (7) Inspection facilities should be built at each dock; (8) Jiang has already built them, but Nanjing is still lacking; (Jiujiang has already built them, but Nanjing is still lacking); (8) Now that it is summer, hygiene facilities should be implemented quickly (the military police, together with the purser, will urge the tea room staff to clean at all times, and more spittoons should be placed, and more disinfectant should be sprayed to prevent epidemics); (9) Order of boarding and disembarking should be strictly maintained (passengers often crowd the sides of the ship before arriving at the shore, blocking traffic; the military police, together with the purser, will stop passengers from rushing and pushing 30 minutes before the ship stops to avoid danger); (10) Ship employees must cooperate with the military police (the military police protecting the ship are closely related to the interests of the ship, so everything should be discussed and handled together, and no prejudice should be allowed to avoid estrangement).

Solar Black Spots are Larger - This Year May Not Be Too Hot - Hurricane Warning Method Changes Next Month - Broadcast by the Central Yangming Institute 113

Regarding hurricane warnings, which are crucial for the safety of shipowners and fishermen, the Ministry of Industry previously consulted the Ministry of Communications to have the Xujiahui Observatory provide free information to the Shanghai Radio Station, which would then relay it to coastal provinces and cities to inform nearby shipowners and fishermen, in order to protect the safety of fishermen in various fishing areas. Now, the Ministry of Communications believes that there are no restrictions on the number of meteorological telegrams sent from various places, which not only congests the lines but also delays them due to repeated forwarding, thus rendering them ineffective. Therefore, it has been decided to change the method on the first of next month. From then on, the Central Yangming Institute will provide Yangming reports and hurricane warnings. Aviation Highway Construction Lottery Tickets - Method Changed for the Thirteenth Issue - Changed to 300,000 Tickets Held Once a Month - First Prize is 250,000, and Other Prizes are Larger 117

The National Government's aviation highway construction lottery tickets have been sold for twelve issues. The office has now presented the Ministry of Finance to change the prize amounts, etc., from the thirteenth issue onwards. The new lottery tickets have been printed and distributed, and the draw is scheduled to be held in Shanghai on August 9th. Afterwards, it will be held once a month. The modified method is recorded below:

Total Number of Lottery Tickets - Changed to 300,000

The total number of lottery tickets was originally 500,000, each costing ten yuan, and sold in ten series. It has now been changed to 300,000, still divided into ten series, and drawn once a month. The winning numbers have been changed as follows: one first prize winner wins 250,000 yuan; four second prize winners win 50,000 yuan each; twenty third prize winners win 10,000 yuan each; one hundred fourth prize winners win 2,000 yuan each; three hundred fifth prize winners win 500 yuan each; six hundred sixth prize winners win 100 yuan each. The upper and lower consecutive numbers of the first prize have two additional prizes, each winning 6,000 yuan; the upper and lower consecutive numbers of the second prize have eight additional prizes, each winning 1,000 yuan; the last two characters of the first prize are the same for 2,999 tickets, each winning 50 yuan; the last character of the first prize is the same for 27,000 tickets, each winning 10 yuan. The total number of winning lottery tickets is 31,034, and the total prize money is 1,499,950 yuan.

Drawing Method - Also Changed

The number of winning numbers has increased, and the drawing method has also changed. There are still two types of prize balls, A and B, from 00 to 299, a total of 3,000. The prize balls for the prize levels are from the first prize to the fourth prize, a total of 125. The prize balls for the fifth and sixth prizes use the B balls. For the fifth prize, one is drawn, and those with the same last three characters win. For the sixth prize, two are drawn, the same as the fifth prize. The remaining additional prizes are based on the numbers of the first and second prizes and are not drawn separately. Therefore, although the prize levels have increased, the drawing method is simple and clear, so as not to prolong the time.

This Issue's Sales - Similar to Before

According to the person in charge of the office, the method of changing the prize numbers has been determined, but it is still striving to be simple and clear so that the audience can understand it at a glance. Also, the unsold lottery tickets from the previous issue were sold by the China Aviation Construction Association. It has not yet been decided whether to follow this method this time. As for the sales volume of this issue, it is similar to previous issues, but there are occasional rumors in the north, so the sales volume is affected. After the change, the sales will definitely increase due to the greater chance of winning.

There are various torsion, friction, fatigue, and other testing machines, as well as the most urgently needed chemical instruments, worth more than 40,000 yuan. After the completion ceremony of the institute, it will begin testing domestic industrial materials and testing various manufactured equipment or materials for manufacturers across the country.

Wujiang Native Place Association - Telegram Requests the Removal of Taihu Lake Enclosure Fields 125

The Wujiang Native Place Association in Shanghai submitted a document to the Jiangsu Provincial Government, saying to Chen, Chairman of the Jiangsu Provincial Government in Zhenjiang, and Shen, Director of the Department of Construction, saying: The country is based on agriculture, and the wealth of Jiangnan is the best in the world, which is actually due to the gift of Taihu Lake. If Taihu Lake loses its effectiveness, then the prosperity of Su will gradually decline. The cheap grain damaged agriculture two years ago, and the severe drought raged last year. The rural areas went bankrupt, and the social economy gradually shrank. This is clear evidence. In drought, the water dries up, so it is appropriate to dredge urgently. The government does not add dredging governance, and the local customers collude, so they made large-scale enclosure fields. The enclosed fields are about 18 li long from north to south and about 6 li wide from east to west, and there are five or six companies. Their offices are all set up in Wujiang. The Wujiang County magistrate patrolled in disguise at the beginning of his tenure to investigate the social situation. How could he have heard nothing about this matter? Until the matter was exposed, the county committee and the gentry and people went to the lake to conduct a field survey, submitted a request to dismantle the enclosure, and then Jiang and Wu counties promoted to the province one after another, and said in person that Wei Tai had clearly ordered that the machine was still under investigation. Now that two sentences have passed, what about the investigation? I have not seen the bulletin. It is rumored that only the Songling Songchang built by the local people is being demolished, and the ones surrounded by the guest people have not been demolished. (Omission) The water conservancy of Taihu Lake is related to the livelihood of the people of Su, Zhejiang, and seven prefectures, and no one can slaughter it, especially a few people who can monopolize it. (Omission) Now check the enclosure fields in Wu County, and most of them have been removed, with no repercussions. However, in Wujiang, when it was first proposed to dismantle it, those people arbitrarily resisted. The background in this is obvious. (Omission) Our chairman and hall leader must consider carefully and treat the symptoms and root causes. However, there is another severe drought this year, and the downstream needs water urgently. If the deep abyss in the lower reaches of Wusong is blocked, it will not be restored, then the move to deepen the Ji mound and dredge the Songjiang will be meaningless. Not only will the farmland transportation in the three prefectures of Su, Song, and Tai be greatly affected, but also. For this reason, I implore your seat to quickly order the Wujiang County magistrate to dismantle all the groups, and order the Jiangnan Water Conservancy Project Office to plan and dredge as soon as possible. Waiting for Mingxun, I can't wait any longer. I respectfully state that the members of the Wujiang Native Place Association in Shanghai, Xu Peihuang, and others kowtow together.

Xing Zhigang Asks Five Provincial Transportation Orders - To Reduce the Shanghai-Minhang Car Price 126

Xing Zhigang and others, citizens of Shanghai County, submitted a document to the Transportation Committee of the five provinces and cities of Su, Zhejiang, Anhui, and Beijing-Shanghai yesterday, saying that the Shanghai-Minhang Automobile Company is holding up the car price and disrespecting the government. They urged the city government to correct it quickly to benefit highway transportation. The document stated: According to the standards of the general rules for passenger transportation by highway vehicles in the five provinces and cities, the price is three cents per person per kilometer. Now, the Shanghai-Minhang Automobile Company charges 75 cents for the entire 29-kilometer journey. In fact, because the round-trip ticket price of the Shanghai-Minhang ship is low, it does not seem to exceed the stipulated car price, holding this to cover up the eyes and ears of the authorities. But if you look at the content, the price from Qianliang Temple to Wujia Lane is 1.5 cents for two kilometers, from Wujia Lane to Huiling Middle School is 1.5 cents for 1.9 kilometers, from Huiling Middle School to Caohejing is 1.5 cents for 1.6 kilometers, and from Caohejing to Tushanwan is 1.5 cents for 1.9 kilometers. When the car is driving, each station is less than three minutes, and each station sells 1.5 cents, which exceeds the stipulated car price by more than half. Only the section from Tushanwan to the Shanghai Local Office, which is 6.4 kilometers, takes 12 minutes, and the fare is 20 cents, which is in line with the standard price. This section is because there is a Longhua car run by the Municipal Public Utilities Bureau nearby. The journey is longer, but it only sells for 480 yuan, which is 1.5 cents, which is in proportion, so the Shanghai-Minhang company cannot increase its price deliberately. The people have repeatedly submitted requests to the municipal authorities to inform the company to reduce the car price in order to develop the traffic on this road and prosper the city. The reply to reduce prices was not obtained. It is found that the Shanghai-Minhang car is the throat of the Shanghai-Hangzhou highway and the lifeline of Shanghai-Minhang commerce. In the autumn of rural bankruptcy, it is very appropriate to abide by the government's order and work together to overcome difficulties. It should not be contrary to the government's intentions and create this deformed car price and be criticized by the local area. The people will ask the council to strictly enforce the order, unify the road rights, develop the enterprises along the road, and for the sake of transportation, especially provide words and earnestly ask your seat to look at the facts, quickly give advice to the Shanghai Municipal Government, and inform the Shanghai-Minhang Automobile Company to abide by the five-province and city highway car passenger transportation rules, quickly reduce the car price, and issue round-trip tickets at each station, which are sold at 70% of the round-trip car price, and add a 12 o'clock bus once to benefit travelers and facilitate transportation. I can't wait any longer.
